{KauśS, 1, 1}
atha vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 1]
sa punar āmnāyapratyayaḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 2]
āmnāyaḥ punar mantrāś ca brāhmaṇāni ca | [KauśS, 1, 1 3]
tad yathābrāhmaṇaṃ vidhir evaṃ karmaliṅgā mantrāḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 4]
tathānyārthaḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 5]
tathā brāhmaṇaliṅgā mantrāḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 6]
tadabhāve saṃpradāyaḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 7]
pramuktatvād brāhmaṇānām | [KauśS, 1, 1 8]
yajñaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 9]
devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca | [KauśS, 1, 1 10]
prāṅmukha upāṃśu karoti | [KauśS, 1, 1 11]
yajñopavītī devānām | [KauśS, 1, 1 12]
prācīnavītī pitṝṇām | [KauśS, 1, 1 13]
prāg udag vā devānām | [KauśS, 1, 1 14]
dakṣiṇā pitṝṇām | [KauśS, 1, 1 15]
prāgudag apavargaṃ devānām | [KauśS, 1, 1 16]
dakṣiṇāpratyag apavargaṃ pitṝṇām | [KauśS, 1, 1 17]
sakṛt karma pitṝṇām | [KauśS, 1, 1 18]
tryavarārdhaṃ devānām | [KauśS, 1, 1 19]
yathādiṣṭaṃ vā | [KauśS, 1, 1 20]
abhidakṣiṇam ācāro devānām | [KauśS, 1, 1 21]
prasavyaṃ pitṝṇām | [KauśS, 1, 1 22]
svāhākāravaṣaṭkārapradānā devāḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 23]
svadhākāranamaskārapradānā pitaraḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 24]
upamūlalūnaṃ barhiḥ pitṝṇām | [KauśS, 1, 1 25]
parvasu devānām | [KauśS, 1, 1 26]
pra yaccha parśum iti darbhāhārāya dātraṃ prayacchati | [KauśS, 1, 1 27]
oṣadhīr dāntu parvan ityupari parvaṇāṃ lūtvā tūṣṇīm āhṛtyottarato 'gner upasādayati | [KauśS, 1, 1 28]
nāgniṃ viparyāvarteta | [KauśS, 1, 1 29]
nāntarā yajñāṅgāni vyaveyāt | [KauśS, 1, 1 30]
dakṣiṇaṃ jānu prabhujya juhoti | [KauśS, 1, 1 31]
yā pūrvā paurṇamāsī sānumatir yottarā sā rākā | [KauśS, 1, 1 32]
yā pūrvāmāvāsyā sā sinīvālī yottarā sā kuhūḥ | [KauśS, 1, 1 33]
adyopavasatha ityupavatsyadbhaktam aśnāti | [KauśS, 1, 1 34]
madhulavaṇamāṃsamāṣavarjam | [KauśS, 1, 1 35]
mamāgne varcaḥ iti samidha ādhāya vratam upaiti | [KauśS, 1, 1 36]
vratena tvāṃ vratapate iti vā | [KauśS, 1, 1 37]
brahmacārī vratī | [KauśS, 1, 1 38]
adhaḥ śayīta | [KauśS, 1, 1 39]
prātarhute 'gnau karmaṇe vāṃ veṣāya vāṃ sukṛtāya vām iti pāṇī prakṣālyāpareṇāgner darbhān āstīrya teṣūttaram ānaḍuhaṃ rohitaṃ carma prāggrīvam uttaraloma prastīrya pavitre kurute | [KauśS, 1, 1 40]
darbhāvaprachinnāntau prakṣālyānulomam anumārṣṭi viṣṇor manasā pūte sthaḥ iti | [KauśS, 1, 1 41]
{KauśS, 1, 2}
tvaṃ bhūmim aty eṣy ojasā tvaṃ vedyāṃ sīdasi cārur adhvare tvāṃ pavitram ṛṣayo bharantas tvaṃ punīhi duritāny asmat iti pavitre antardhāya havir nirvapati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 1]
evam agniṣomābhyām iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 2]
indrāgnibhyām ityamāvāsyāyām | [KauśS, 1, 2 3]
nityaṃ pūrvam āgneyam | [KauśS, 1, 2 4]
niruptaṃ pavitrābhyāṃ prokṣati amuṣmai tvā juṣṭam yathādevatam | [KauśS, 1, 2 5]
ulūkhalamusalaṃ śūrpaṃ prakṣālitaṃ carmaṇyādhāya vrīhīn ulūkhala opyāvaghnaṃs trir haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjati haviṣkṛd ā dravehi iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 6]
avahatya suphalīkṛtān kṛtvā triḥ prakṣālya taṇḍulān agne varur yajñiyas tvādhi arukṣat iti carum adhidadhāti | [KauśS, 1, 2 7]
śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ ityudakam āsiñcati | [KauśS, 1, 2 8]
brahmaṇā śuddhāḥ iti taṇḍulān | [KauśS, 1, 2 9]
pari tvāgne puraṃ vayam iti triḥ paryagni karoti | [KauśS, 1, 2 10]
nekṣaṇena triḥ pradakṣiṇam udāyauti | [KauśS, 1, 2 11]
ata ūrdhvaṃ yathākāmam | [KauśS, 1, 2 12]
uttarato 'gner upasādayatīdhmam | [KauśS, 1, 2 13]
uttaraṃ barhiḥ | [KauśS, 1, 2 14]
agnaye tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi itīdhmam | [KauśS, 1, 2 15]
pṛthivyai iti barhiḥ | [KauśS, 1, 2 16]
darbhamuṣṭim abhyukṣya paścād agneḥ prāgagraṃ nidadhāti ūrṇamradaṃ prathasva svāsasthaṃ devebhyaḥ iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 17]
darbhāṇām apādāya ṛṣīṇāṃ prastaro 'si iti dakṣiṇato 'gner brahmāsanaṃ nidadhāti | [KauśS, 1, 2 18]
purastād agner āstīrya teṣāṃ mūlānyapareṣāṃ prāntair avacchādayan parisarpati dakṣiṇenāgnim ā paścārdhāt | [KauśS, 1, 2 19]
pari stṛṇīhi iti sampreṣyati | [KauśS, 1, 2 20]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ prasūtaḥ praśiṣā paristṛṇāmi iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 21]
evam uttarato 'yujo dhātūn kurvan | [KauśS, 1, 2 22]
yatra samāgacchanti tad dakṣiṇottaraṃ kṛṇoti | [KauśS, 1, 2 23]
stīrṇaṃ prokṣati haviṣāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 24]
nānabhyukṣitaṃ saṃstīrṇam upayogaṃ labheta | [KauśS, 1, 2 25]
naidho'bhyādānam | [KauśS, 1, 2 26]
nānutpūtaṃ haviḥ | [KauśS, 1, 2 27]
nāprokṣitaṃ yajñāṅgam | [KauśS, 1, 2 28]
tasmin prakṣālitopavātāni nidadhāti | [KauśS, 1, 2 29]
sruvam ājyadhānīṃ ca | [KauśS, 1, 2 30]
vilīnapūtam ājyaṃ gṛhītvādhiśritya paryagni kṛtvodag udvāsya paścād agner upasādyodagagrābhyāṃ pavitrābhyām utpunāti | [KauśS, 1, 2 31]
viṣṇor manasā pūtam asi | [KauśS, 1, 2 32]
devas tvā savitot punātu | [KauśS, 1, 2 33]
acchidreṇa tvā pavitreṇa śatadhāreṇa sahasradhāreṇa supvot punāmi iti tṛtīyam | [KauśS, 1, 2 34]
tūṣṇīṃ caturtham | [KauśS, 1, 2 35]
śṛtaṃ havir abhighārayati madhvā samañjan ghṛtavat karātha iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 36]
abhighāryodañcam udvāsayati ud vāsayāgneḥ śṛtam akarma havyam ā sīda pṛṣṭham amṛtasya dhāma iti | [KauśS, 1, 2 37]
paścād ājyasya nidhāyālaṃkṛtya samānenotpunāti | [KauśS, 1, 2 38]
adārasṛt ityavekṣate | [KauśS, 1, 2 39]
ut tiṣṭhata ityaindram | [KauśS, 1, 2 40]
agnir bhūyām iti tisṛbhir upasamādadhāti asmai kṣatrāṇi etam idhmam iti vā | [KauśS, 1, 2 41]
{KauśS, 1, 3}
yunajmi tvā brahmaṇā daivyena havyāyāsmai voḍheva jātavedaḥ indhānās tvā suprajasaḥ suvīrā jyog jīvema balihṛto vayaṃ te iti | [KauśS, 1, 3 1]
dakṣiṇato jāṅmāyanam udapātram upasādyābhimantrayate tathodapātraṃ dhāraya yathāgre brahmaṇaspatiḥ satyadharmā adīdharad devasya savituḥ save iti | [KauśS, 1, 3 2]
athodakam āsiñcati iheta devīr amṛtaṃ vasānā hiraṇyavarṇā anavadyarūpāḥ āpaḥ samudro varuṇaś ca rājā saṃpātabhāgān haviṣo juṣantām indrapraśiṣṭā varuṇaprasūtā apaḥ samudrād divam ud vahantu indrapraśiṣṭā varuṇaprasūtā divas pṛthivyā śriyam ud vahantu iti | [KauśS, 1, 3 3]
ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmi jātavedaḥ iti saha havirbhiḥ paryukṣya jīvābhir ācamyotthāya vedaprapadbhiḥ prapadyata oṃ prapadye bhūḥ prapadye bhuvaḥ prapadye svaḥ prapadye janat prapadye iti | [KauśS, 1, 3 4]
prapadya paścāt stīrṇasya darbhān āstīrya ahe daidhiṣavyod atas tiṣṭhāny asya sadane sīda yo 'smat pākatara iti brahmāsanam anvīkṣate | [KauśS, 1, 3 5]
nirastaḥ parāgvasuḥ saha pāpmanā nirastaḥ so 'stu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇā tṛṇaṃ nirasyati | [KauśS, 1, 3 6]
tad anvālabhya japati idam aham arvāgvasoḥ sadane sīdāmyṛtasya sadane sīdāmi satyasya sadane sīdāmīṣṭasya sadane sīdāmi pūrtasya sadane sīdāmi māmṛṣad deva barhiḥ svāsasthaṃ tvādhyāsadeyam ūrṇamradam anabhiśokam | [KauśS, 1, 3 7]
vimṛgvarīṃ ityupaviśyāsanīyaṃ brahmajapaṃ japati bṛhaspatir brahmā brahmasadana āsiṣyate bṛhaspate yajñaṃ gopāya yad ud udvata un nivataḥ śakeyam iti | [KauśS, 1, 3 8]
darbhaiḥ sruvaṃ nirmṛjya niṣṭaptaṃ rakṣo niṣṭaptā arātayaḥ pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātayaḥ iti pratapya mūle sruvaṃ gṛhītvā japati viṣṇor hasto 'si dakṣiṇaḥ pūṣṇā datto bṛhaspateḥ taṃ tvāhaṃ sruvam ā dade devānāṃ havyavāhanam ayaṃ sruvo vi dadhāti homān śatākṣarachandasā jāgatena sarvā yajñasya samanakti viṣṭhā bārhaspatyeṣṭiḥ śarmaṇā daivyena iti | [KauśS, 1, 3 9]
oṃ bhūḥ śaṃ bhūtyai tvā gṛhṇe bhūtaye iti prathamaṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇāti | [KauśS, 1, 3 10]
oṃ bhuvaḥ śaṃ puṣṭyai tvā gṛhṇe puṣṭaye iti dvitīyam | [KauśS, 1, 3 11]
oṃ svaḥ śaṃ tvā gṛhṇe sahasrapoṣāya iti tṛtīyam | [KauśS, 1, 3 12]
oṃ jagacchaṃ tvā gṛhṇe 'parimitapoṣāya iti caturtham | [KauśS, 1, 3 13]
rājakarmābhicārikeṣu amuṣya tvā prāṇāya gṛhṇe 'pānāya vyānāya samānāyodānāya iti pañcamam | [KauśS, 1, 3 14]
agnāv agniḥ hṛdā pūtam purastād yuktaḥ yajñasya cakṣuḥ iti juhoti | [KauśS, 1, 3 15]
paścād agner madhyadeśe samānatra purastāddhomān | [KauśS, 1, 3 16]
dakṣiṇenāgnim udapātra ājyāhutīnāṃ saṃpātān ānayati | [KauśS, 1, 3 17]
purastāddhoma ājyabhāgaḥ saṃsthitahomaḥ samṛddhiḥ śāntānām | [KauśS, 1, 3 18]
ityetāvājyabhāgau | [KauśS, 1, 3 19]
{KauśS, 1, 4}
vṛṣṇe bṛhate svarvide agnaye śulkaṃ harāmi tviṣīmate sa na sthirān balavataḥ kṛṇotu jyok ca no jīvātave dadhāti agnaye svāhā ityuttarapūrvārdha āgneyam ājyabhāgaṃ juhoti | [KauśS, 1, 4 1]
dakṣiṇapūrvārdhe somāya tvaṃ soma divyo nṛcakṣāḥ sugāṁ asmabhyaṃ patho anu khyaḥ abhi no gotraṃ viduṣa iva neṣo 'cchā no vācam uśatīṃ jigāsi somāya svāhā iti | [KauśS, 1, 4 2]
madhye haviḥ | [KauśS, 1, 4 3]
upastīryājyaṃ saṃhatābhyām aṅgulibhyāṃ dvir haviṣo 'vadyati madhyāt pūrvārdhācca | [KauśS, 1, 4 4]
avattam abhighārya dvir haviḥ pratyabhighārayati | [KauśS, 1, 4 5]
yato yato 'vadyati tad anupūrvam | [KauśS, 1, 4 6]
evaṃ sarvāṇyavadānāni | [KauśS, 1, 4 7]
anyatra sauviṣṭakṛtāt | [KauśS, 1, 4 8]
ud enam uttaraṃ naya iti purastāddhomasaṃhatāṃ pūrvām | [KauśS, 1, 4 9]
evaṃ pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ saṃhatāṃ juhoti | [KauśS, 1, 4 10]
svāhāntābhiḥ pratyṛcaṃ homāḥ | [KauśS, 1, 4 11]
yām uttarām agner ājyabhāgasya juhoti rakṣodevatyā sā yāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ somasya pitṛdevatyā sā | [KauśS, 1, 4 12]
tasmād antarā hotavyā devaloka eva hūyante | [KauśS, 1, 4 13]
yāṃ hutvā pūrvām aparāṃ juhoti sāpakramantī sa pāpīyān yajamāno bhavati | [KauśS, 1, 4 14]
yāṃ parāṃ parāṃ saṃhatāṃ juhoti sābhikramantī sa vasīyān yajamāno bhavati | [KauśS, 1, 4 15]
yām anagnau juhoti sāndhā tayā cakṣur yajamānasya mīyate so 'ndhaṃbhāvuko yajamāno bhavati | [KauśS, 1, 4 16]
yāṃ dhūme juhoti sā tamasi hūyate so 'rocako yajamāno bhavati | [KauśS, 1, 4 17]
yāṃ jyotiṣmati juhoti tayā brahmavarcasī bhavati tasmājjyotiṣmati hotavyam | [KauśS, 1, 4 18]
evam asmai kṣatram agnīṣomau ityagniṣomīyasya | [KauśS, 1, 4 19]
{KauśS, 1, 5}
agnīṣomā savedasā sahūtī vanataṃ giraḥ sa devatrā babhūvathuḥ yuvam etāni divi rocanāny agniś ca soma sakratū adhattam yuvaṃ sindhūṃr abhiśaster avadyād agnīṣomāv amuñcataṃ gṛbhītān agnīṣomā ya āhutiṃ yo vāṃ dāśāddhaviṣkṛtim sa prajayā suvīryaṃ viśvam āyur vyaśnavat | [KauśS, 1, 5 1]
indrāgnī rocanā divaḥ pari vājeṣu bhūṣathaḥ tad vāṃ ceti pra vīryam śnathad vṛtram uta sanoti vājam indrā yo agnī sahurī saparyāt irajyantā vasavyasya bhūreḥ sahastamā sahasā vājayantā indrāgnī asmān rakṣatāṃ yau prajānāṃ prajāvatī sa prajayā suvīryaṃ viśvam āyur vyaśnavat gomaddhiraṇyavad vasu yad vām aśvāvad īmahe indrāgnī vanemahi svāhā iti | [KauśS, 1, 5 2]
aindrāgnasya haviṣo 'māvāsyāyām | [KauśS, 1, 5 3]
prāk sviṣṭakṛtaḥ pārvaṇahomau samṛddhihomāḥ kāmyahomāś ca | [KauśS, 1, 5 4]
pūrṇā paścāt iti paurṇamāsyām | [KauśS, 1, 5 5]
yat te devā akṛṇvan bhāgadheyam ityamāvāsyāyām | [KauśS, 1, 5 6]
ākūtyai tvā svāhā kāmāya tvā svāhā samṛdhe tvā svāhā ākūtyai tvā kāmāya tvā samṛdhe tvā svāhā ṛcā stomaṃ samardhaya gāyatreṇa rathantaraṃ bṛhad gāyatravartani svāhā | [KauśS, 1, 5 7]
pṛthivyām agnaye samanaman iti saṃnatibhiś ca prajāpate na tvad etāny anyaḥ iti ca | [KauśS, 1, 5 8]
upastīryājyaṃ sarveṣām uttarataḥ sakṛtsakṛd avadāya dvir avattam abhighārayati | [KauśS, 1, 5 9]
na havīṃṣi | [KauśS, 1, 5 10]
ā devānām api panthām aganma yacchaknavāma tad anupravoḍhum agnir vidvān sa yajāt sa iddhotā so 'dhvarān sa ṛtūn kalpayāti agnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā ity uttarapūrvārdhe 'vayutaṃ hutvā sarvaprāyaścittīyān homāñjuhoti | [KauśS, 1, 5 11]
svāheṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍ aniṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā bheṣajaṃ sviṣṭyai svāhā niṣkṛtir duriṣṭyai svāhā daivībhyas tanūbhyaḥ svāhā ayāś cāgne 'sy anabhiśastiś ca satyam it tvam ayā asi ayāsā manasā kṛto 'yās san havyam ūhiṣe ā no dhehi bheṣajam svāhā iti oṃ svāhā bhūḥ svāhā bhuvaḥ svāhā svaḥ svāhoṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā iti | [KauśS, 1, 5 12]
{KauśS, 1, 6}
yan me skannaṃ manaso jātavedo yad vāskandaddhaviṣo yatra yatra utpruṣo vipruṣaḥ saṃ juhomi satyāḥ santu yajamānasya kāmāḥ svāhā iti | [KauśS, 1, 6 1]
yan me skannaṃ yad asmṛti iti ca skannāsmṛtihomau | [KauśS, 1, 6 2]
yad adya tvā prayati iti saṃsthitahomāḥ | [KauśS, 1, 6 3]
manasas pate iti uttamaṃ caturgṛhītena | [KauśS, 1, 6 4]
barhir ājyaśeṣe 'nakti | [KauśS, 1, 6 5]
pṛthivyai tvā iti mūlam antarikṣāya tvā iti madhyaṃ dive tvā iti agram evaṃ triḥ | [KauśS, 1, 6 6]
saṃ barhir aktam ity anupraharati yathādevatam | [KauśS, 1, 6 7]
sruvam agnau dhārayati | [KauśS, 1, 6 8]
yad ājyadhānyāṃ tat saṃsrāvayati saṃsrāvabhāgās taviṣā bṛhantaḥ prastareṣṭhā barhiṣadaś ca devāḥ imaṃ yajñam abhi viśve gṛṇantaḥ svāhā devā amṛtā mādayantām iti | [KauśS, 1, 6 9]
sruvo 'si ghṛtād aniśitaḥ sapatnakṣayaṇo divi ṣīda antarikṣe sīda pṛthivyāṃ sīdottaro 'haṃ bhūyāsam adhare matsapatnāḥ iti sruvaṃ prāgdaṇḍaṃ nidadhāti | [KauśS, 1, 6 10]
vi muñcāmi brahmaṇā jātavedasam agniṃ hotāram ajaraṃ rathaspṛtam sarvā devānāṃ janimāni vidvān yathābhāgaṃ vahatu havyam agniḥ agnaye svāhā iti samidham ādadhāti | [KauśS, 1, 6 11]
edho 'si iti dvitīyāṃ samid asi iti tṛtīyam | [KauśS, 1, 6 12]
tejo 'si iti mukhaṃ vimārṣṭi | [KauśS, 1, 6 13]
dakṣiṇenāgniṃ trīn viṣṇukramān kramate viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si iti dakṣiṇena pādenānusaṃharati savyam | [KauśS, 1, 6 14]
sūryasyāvṛtam ity abhidakṣiṇam āvartate | [KauśS, 1, 6 15]
aganma svaḥ ity ādityam īkṣate | [KauśS, 1, 6 16]
indrasya vacasā vayaṃ mitrasya varuṇasya ca brahmaṇā sthāpitaṃ pātraṃ punar utthāpayāmasi ity apareṇāgnim udapātraṃ parihṛtyottareṇāgnim āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ iti mārjayitvā barhiṣi patnyāñjalau ninayati samudraṃ vaḥ pra hiṇomi iti idaṃ janāsaḥ iti vā | [KauśS, 1, 6 17]
vīrapatny ahaṃ bhūyāsam iti mukhaṃ vimārṣṭi | [KauśS, 1, 6 18]

{KauśS, 7, 7}

tataḥ saṃhitām | [KauśS, 7, 7 11.1]

{KauśS, 7, 8}

saumyaṃ tanvacchyāmākaṃ śaradi | [KauśS, 9, 6 16.1]

{KauśS, 11, 8}

śirograhaṃ paricakṣate | [KauśS, 11, 8 13]

avāgaṅguriṃ parvamātrīm ity eke | [KauśS, 11, 8 15]

ihaivaidhi dhanasanir ity ekaṃ hṛtvā | [KauśS, 11, 8 21]

saṃbhārān upasādayati | [KauśS, 11, 8 23]
paryukṣaṇīṃ barhir udakumbhaṃ kaṃsaṃ darvim ājyam āyavanaṃ caruṃ vāsāṃsy āñjanam abhyañjanam iti | [KauśS, 11, 8 24]

ato yajñopavītī pitryupavītī barhir gṛhītvā vicṛtya saṃnahanaṃ dakṣiṇāparam aṣṭamadeśam abhyavāsyet | [KauśS, 11, 8 26]

āyāpanādīni trīṇi | [KauśS, 11, 8 28]

paryukṣya | [KauśS, 11, 8 31]
{KauśS, 11, 9}

amīmadanta patnyo yathābhāgaṃ yathālokam āvṛṣāyiṣateti | [KauśS, 11, 9 22.1]
āpo agnim ity adbhir agnim avasicya | [KauśS, 11, 9 23.1]

{KauśS, 11, 10}

{KauśS, 12, 1}

{KauśS, 12, 2}

{KauśS, 12, 3}

tān pratimantrayate | [KauśS, 12, 3 13.1]

atisṛjati | [KauśS, 12, 3 14.1]

oṃ tṛṇāni gaur attv iti āha | [KauśS, 12, 3 14.4]
sūyavasād iti pratiṣṭhamānām anumantrayate | [KauśS, 12, 3 15.1]
nālohito madhuparko bhavati | [KauśS, 12, 3 16.1]

āgneyīṃ vapāṃ kuryuḥ | [KauśS, 12, 3 20.1]

athāsmai snānam anulepanaṃ mālābhyañjanam iti | [KauśS, 12, 3 22.1]
yad atropasamāhāryaṃ bhavati tad upasamāhṛtya | [KauśS, 12, 3 23.1]
athopāsakāḥ prāyopāsakāḥ smo bho iti vedayante | [KauśS, 12, 3 24.1]
tān pratimantrayate | [KauśS, 12, 3 25.1]
bhūyāṃso bhūyāsma ye ca no bhūyasaḥ kārṣṭāpi ca no 'nye bhūyāṃso jāyantām | [KauśS, 12, 3 25.2]
asya ca dātur iti dātāram īkṣate | [KauśS, 12, 3 26.1]

tān pratimantrayate | [KauśS, 12, 3 28.1]

asya ca dātur iti dātāram īkṣate | [KauśS, 12, 3 29.1]

{KauśS, 13, 2}
atha yatraitāni varṣāṇi varṣanti ghṛtaṃ māṃsaṃ madhu ca yaddhiraṇyaṃ yāni cāpyanyāni ghorāṇi varṣāṇi varṣanti tat parābhavati kulaṃ vā grāmo vā janapado vā | [KauśS, 13, 2 1.1]

sa āhopakalpayadhvam iti | [KauśS, 13, 2 5.1]

api ced eva yadā kadācid ārtāya kuryāt | [KauśS, 13, 2 8.1]
snāto 'hatavasanaḥ surabhir vratavān karmaṇya upavasatyekarātraṃ trirātraṃ ṣaḍrātraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ vā | [KauśS, 13, 2 9.1]
dvādaśyāḥ prātar yatraivādaḥ patitaṃ bhavati tata uttaram agnim upasamādhāya | [KauśS, 13, 2 10.1]
parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhir udapātram upasādya paricaraṇenājyaṃ paricarya | [KauśS, 13, 2 11.1]
nityān purastāddhomān hutvājyabhāgau ca | [KauśS, 13, 2 12.1]
atha juhoti | [KauśS, 13, 2 13.1]
ghṛtasya dhārā iha yā varṣanti pakvaṃ māṃsaṃ madhu ca yaddhiraṇyam | [KauśS, 13, 2 14.1]
dviṣantam etā anuyantu vṛṣṭayo 'pāṃ vṛṣṭayo bahulāḥ santu mahyam | [KauśS, 13, 2 14.2]

agnaye svāheti hutvā | [KauśS, 13, 2 14.5]
divyo gandharva iti mātṛnāmabhir juhuyāt | [KauśS, 13, 2 15.1]

sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [KauśS, 13, 2 18.1]
{KauśS, 13, 3}

varam anaḍvāham iti samānam | [KauśS, 13, 5 9.1]

indro no astu purogavaḥ sa no rakṣatu sarvataḥ | [KauśS, 13, 12 2.3]
indrāya svāheti hutvā | [KauśS, 13, 12 2.4]

sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [KauśS, 13, 12 4.1]
{KauśS, 13, 13}
atha yatraitad daivatāni nṛtyanti cyotanti hasanti gāyanti vānyāni vā rūpāṇi kurvanti ya āsurā manuṣyā mā no vidan namo devavadhebhya iti abhayair juhuyāt | [KauśS, 13, 13 1.1]
sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [KauśS, 13, 13 2.1]
{KauśS, 13, 14}
atha yatraitallāṅgale saṃsṛjataḥ puroḍāśaṃ śrapayitvā | [KauśS, 13, 14 1.1]
araṇyasyārdham abhivrajya | [KauśS, 13, 14 2.1]
prācīṃ sītāṃ sthāpayitvā | [KauśS, 13, 14 3.1]
sītāyā madhye prāñcam idhmam upasamādhāya | [KauśS, 13, 14 4.1]

atha juhoti | [KauśS, 13, 14 6.1]
vittir asi puṣṭir asi śrīr asi prājāpatyānāṃ tāṃ tvāhaṃ mayi puṣṭikāmo juhomi svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 14 6.2]
kumudvatī puṣkariṇī sītā sarvāṅgaśobhanī | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.1]
kṛṣiḥ sahasraprakārā pratyaṣṭā śrīr iyaṃ mayi | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.2]
urvīṃ tvāhur manuṣyāḥ śriyaṃ tvā manaso viduḥ | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.3]
āśaye 'nnasya no dhehy anamīvasya śuṣmiṇaḥ | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.4]
parjanyapatni hariṇyabhijitāsy abhi no vada | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.5]
kālanetre haviṣo no juṣasva tṛptiṃ no dhehi dvipade catuṣpade | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.6]
yābhir devā asurān akalpayan yātūn manūn gandharvān rākṣasāṃś ca | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.7]
tābhir no adya sumanā upāgahi sahasrāpoṣaṃ subhage rarāṇā | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.8]
hiraṇyasrakpuṣkariṇī śyāmā sarvāṅgaśobhanī | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.9]
kṛṣir hiraṇyaprakārā pratyaṣṭā śrīr iyaṃ mayi | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.10]
aśvibhyāṃ devi saha saṃvidānā indreṇa rādhena saha puṣṭyā na āgahi | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.11]
viśas tvā rāsantāṃ pradiśo 'nu sarvā ahorātrārdhamāsamāsā ārtavā ṛtubhiḥ saha | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.12]
bhartrī devānām uta martyānāṃ bhartrī prajānām uta mānuṣāṇām | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.13]
hastibhir itarāsaiḥ kṣetrasārathibhiḥ saha | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.14]
hiraṇyair aśvair ā gobhiḥ pratyaṣṭā śrīr iyaṃ mayi | [KauśS, 13, 14 7.15]
atra śunāsīrāṇy anuyojayet | [KauśS, 13, 14 8.1]
varam anaḍvāham iti samānam | [KauśS, 13, 14 9.1]
{KauśS, 13, 15}

{KauśS, 13, 16}

{KauśS, 13, 24}

{KauśS, 13, 25}

{KauśS, 13, 32}

sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [KauśS, 13, 32 7.1]
{KauśS, 13, 33}

{KauśS, 13, 34}

{KauśS, 13, 35}

{KauśS, 13, 36}

{KauśS, 13, 41}

{KauśS, 13, 43}
atha yatraitad vaṃśa sphoṭati kapāle 'ṅgārā bhavantyudapātraṃ barhir ājyaṃ tad ādāya | [KauśS, 13, 43 1.1]
śālāyāḥ pṛṣṭham upasarpati | [KauśS, 13, 43 2.1]

uttamarātrī nāma mṛtyo te mātā tasya te antakaḥ pitā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.3]

yābhir vaṃśān abhinidadhāti prāṇināṃ yān kāṃścemān prāṇabhṛtāṃ jighāṃsan | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.6]
sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ mṛtyave svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.7]
bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso brahmaṇaḥ putro viśve devāḥ pradadur viśvam ejat | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.8]
sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ bṛhaspataya āṅgirasāya svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.9]
yasya te 'nnaṃ na kṣīyate bhūya evopajāyate | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.10]
yasmai bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca sarvam etat pratiṣṭhitam | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.11]
sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam indrāya svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.12]
mukhaṃ devānām iha yo babhūva yo jānāti vayunānāṃ samīpe | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.13]
yasmai hutaṃ devatā bhakṣayanti vāyunetraḥ supraṇītiḥ sunītiḥ | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.14]
sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam agnaye svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.15]
yaḥ pṛthivyāṃ cyāvayann eti vṛkṣān prabhañjanena rathena saha saṃvidānaḥ | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.16]
rasān gandhān bhāvayann eti devo mātariśvā bhūtabhavyasya kartā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.17]
sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ vāyave svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.18]
brahmacārī carati brahmacaryam ṛcaṃ gāthāṃ brahma paraṃ jigāṃsan | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.19]
taṃ vighnā anupariyanti sarve ye antarikṣe ye ca divi śritāsaḥ | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.20]
taṃ viśo anuparyanti sarvāḥ karmāṇi loke parimohayanti | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.21]
sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam ādityāya svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.22]
yo nakṣatraiḥ sarathaṃ yāti devaḥ saṃsiddhena rathena saha saṃvidānaḥ | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.23]
rūpaṃ rūpaṃ kṛṇvānaś citrabhānuḥ subhānuḥ | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.24]
sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ candrāya svāhā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.25]
oṣadhayaḥ somarājñīr yaśasvinīḥ | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.26]

yo vanaspatīnām upatāpo babhūva yad vā gṛhān ghoram utājagāma tan nirjagāma haviṣā ghṛtena śaṃ no astu dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.32]

tvaṣṭre svāheti hutvā | [KauśS, 13, 43 9.35]

{KauśS, 13, 44}

vi mimīṣva payasvatīm iti mimānam anumantrayate | [KauśS, 14, 1 10.1]

yat te ūnam iti saṃvapati | [KauśS, 14, 1 13.1]

asaṃbādhaṃ badhyato mānavānām iti prathayati | [KauśS, 14, 1 16.1]

devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyām ā dada iti lekhanam ādāya yatrāgniṃ nidhāsyan bhavati tatra lakṣaṇaṃ karoti | [KauśS, 14, 1 18.1]

aparās tisro madhye | [KauśS, 14, 1 21.1]
tasyāṃ vrīhiyavāv opya | [KauśS, 14, 1 22.1]

tvām agne bhṛgavo nayantām aṅgirasaḥ sadanaṃ śreya ehi | [KauśS, 14, 1 25.2]

bhadraśreyaḥsvastyā vā | [KauśS, 14, 1 26.1]
agne prehīti vā | [KauśS, 14, 1 27.1]
viśvaṃbharā vasudhānī pratiṣṭheti lakṣaṇe pratiṣṭhāpya | [KauśS, 14, 1 28.1]
athedhmam upasamādadhāti | [KauśS, 14, 1 29.1]
agnir bhūmyām oṣadhīṣv agnir diva ā tapaty agnivāsāḥ pṛthivy asitajñūr etam idhmaṃ samāhitaṃ juṣāṇo 'smai kṣatrāṇi dhārayantam agna iti pañcabhi staraṇam | [KauśS, 14, 1 30.1]
ata ūrdhvaṃ barhiṣaḥ | [KauśS, 14, 1 31.1]
tvaṃ bhūmim aty eṣy ojaseti darbhān samprokṣya | [KauśS, 14, 1 32.1]
ṛṣīṇāṃ prastaro 'sīti dakṣiṇato 'gner brahmāsanaṃ nidadhāti | [KauśS, 14, 1 33.1]
purastād agner udak saṃstṛṇāti | [KauśS, 14, 1 34.1]
tathā pratyak | [KauśS, 14, 1 35.1]
pradakṣiṇaṃ barhiṣāṃ mūlāni chādayantottarasyā vediśroṇeḥ pūrvottarataḥ saṃsthāpya | [KauśS, 14, 1 36.1]
ahe daidhiṣavyod atas tiṣṭhāny asya sadane sīda yo 'smat pākatara iti brahmāsanam anvīkṣate | [KauśS, 14, 1 37.1]
nirastaḥ parāgvasuḥ saha pāpmanā nirastaḥ so 'stu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇā tṛṇaṃ nirasyati | [KauśS, 14, 1 38.1]
tad anvālabhya japatīdam aham arvāgvasoḥ sadane sīdāmy ṛtasya sadane sīdāmi satyasya sadane sīdāmīṣṭasya sadane sīdāmi pūrtasya sadane sīdāmi māmṛṣad eva barhiḥ svāsasthaṃ tvādhyāsadeyam ūrṇamradam anabhiśokam | [KauśS, 14, 1 39.1]
vimṛgvarīm ity upaviśyāsanīyaṃ brahmajapaṃ japati bṛhaspatir brahmā brahmasadana āsiṣyate bṛhaspate yajñaṃ gopāya yad ud udvata un nivataḥ śakeyam | [KauśS, 14, 1 40.1]
pātaṃ mā dyāvāpṛthivī aghān na iti dyāvāpṛthivyau samīkṣate | [KauśS, 14, 1 41.1]

vyākhyātaṃ sarvapākayajñiyaṃ tantram | [KauśS, 14, 1 43.1]
{KauśS, 14, 2}
aṣṭakāyām aṣṭakāhomāñ juhuyāt | [KauśS, 14, 2 1]
tasyā havīṃṣi dhānāḥ karambhaḥ śaṣkulyaḥ puroḍāśa udaudanaḥ kṣīraudanas tilaudano yathopapādipaśuḥ | [KauśS, 14, 2 2]
sarveṣāṃ haviṣāṃ samuddhṛtya | [KauśS, 14, 2 3]
darvyā juhuyāt prathamā ha vy uvāsa seti pañcabhiḥ | [KauśS, 14, 2 4]
āyam agan saṃvatsara iti catasṛbhir vijñāyate | [KauśS, 14, 2 5]
ṛtubhyas tveti vigrāham aṣṭau | [KauśS, 14, 2 6]
indraputra ity aṣṭādaśīm | [KauśS, 14, 2 7]
ahorātrābhyām ity ūnaviṃśīm | [KauśS, 14, 2 8]
paśāv upapadyamāne dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ nirlomaṃ sacarmaṃ sakhuraṃ prakṣālya | [KauśS, 14, 2 9]
iḍāyās padam iti dvābhyāṃ viṃśīm | [KauśS, 14, 2 10]
anupadyamāna ājyaṃ juhuyāt | [KauśS, 14, 2 11]
haviṣāṃ darviṃ pūrayitvā pūrṇā darva iti sadarvīm ekaviṃśīm | [KauśS, 14, 2 12]
ekaviṃśatisaṃstho yajño vijñāyate | [KauśS, 14, 2 13]
sarvā eva yajñatanūr avarunddhe sarvā evāsya yajñatanūḥ pitaram upajīvanti ya evam aṣṭakām upaiti | [KauśS, 14, 2 14]
na darvihome na hastahome na pūrṇahome tantraṃ kriyetety eke | [KauśS, 14, 2 15]
aṣṭakāyāṃ kriyetetīṣuphālimāṭharau | [KauśS, 14, 2 16]
{KauśS, 14, 3}
abhijiti śiṣyān upanīya śvo bhūte saṃbhārān saṃbharati | [KauśS, 14, 3 1.1]
dadhisaktūn pālāśaṃ daṇḍam ahate vasane śuddham ājyaṃ śāntā oṣadhīr navam udakumbham | [KauśS, 14, 3 2.1]
bāhyataḥ śāntavṛkṣasyedhmaṃ prāñcam upasamādhāya | [KauśS, 14, 3 3.1]
parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhir udapātram upasādya paricaraṇenājyaṃ paricarya | [KauśS, 14, 3 4.1]
nityān purastāddhomān hutvājyabhāgau ca | [KauśS, 14, 3 5.1]
paścād agner dadhisaktūñ juhotyagnaye brahmaprajāpatibhyāṃ bhṛgvaṅgirobhya uśanase kāvyāya | [KauśS, 14, 3 6.1]
tato 'bhayair aparājitair gaṇakarmabhir viśvakarmabhir āyuṣyaiḥ svastyayanair ājyaṃ juhuyāt | [KauśS, 14, 3 7.1]
mā no devā ahir vadhīd arasasya śarkoṭasyendrasya prathamo ratho yas te sarpo vṛścikas tṛṣṭadaṃśmā namas te astu vidyuta āre 'sāv asmad astu yas te pṛthu stanayitnur iti saṃsthāpya homān | [KauśS, 14, 3 8.1]
pratiṣṭhāpya sruvaṃ dadhisaktūn prāśyācamyodakam upasamārabhante | [KauśS, 14, 3 9.1]
avyacasaś ceti japitvā sāvitrīṃ brahma jajñānam ity ekāṃ triṣaptīyaṃ ca paccho vācayet | [KauśS, 14, 3 10.1]
śeṣam anuvākasya japanti | [KauśS, 14, 3 11.1]
yo yo bhogaḥ kartavyo bhavati taṃ taṃ kurvate | [KauśS, 14, 3 12.1]
sa khalv etaṃ pakṣam apakṣīyamāṇaḥ pakṣam adhīyāna upaśrāmyetā darśāt | [KauśS, 14, 3 13.1]
dṛṣṭe candramasi phalgunīṣu dvayān rasān upasādayati | [KauśS, 14, 3 14.1]
viśve devā ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ siṃhe vyāghre yaśo havir yaśasaṃ mendro girāv arāgarāṭeṣu yathā somaḥ prātaḥsavane yac ca varco akṣeṣu yena mahānaghnyā jaghanaṃ svāhety agnau hutvā | [KauśS, 14, 3 15.1]
raseṣu saṃpātān ānīya saṃsthāpya homān | [KauśS, 14, 3 16.1]
tata etān prāśayati rasān madhu ghṛtāñchiṣyān | [KauśS, 14, 3 17.1]
yo yo bhogaḥ kartavyo bhavati taṃ taṃ kurvate | [KauśS, 14, 3 18.1]
nānyata āgatāñ śiṣyān parigṛhṇīyāt parasaṃdīkṣitatvāt | [KauśS, 14, 3 19.1]
trirātronāṃścaturo māsāñchiṣyebhyaḥ prabrūyād ardhapañcamān vā | [KauśS, 14, 3 20.1]
pādaṃ pūrvarātre 'dhīyānaḥ pādam apararātre madhyarātre svapan | [KauśS, 14, 3 21.1]
abhuktvā pūrvarātre 'dhīyāna ity eke | [KauśS, 14, 3 22.1]
yathāśaktyapararātre duṣparimāṇo ha pādaḥ | [KauśS, 14, 3 23.1]
pauṣasyāparapakṣe trirātraṃ nādhīyīta | [KauśS, 14, 3 24.1]
tṛtīyasyāḥ prātaḥ samāsaṃ saṃdiśya yasmāt kośād ity antaḥ | [KauśS, 14, 3 25.1]
yasmāt kośād udabharāma vedaṃ tasminn antar ava dadhma enam | [KauśS, 14, 3 26.1]
adhītam iṣṭaṃ brahmaṇo vīryeṇa tena mā devās tapasāvateheti | [KauśS, 14, 3 26.2]
yo yo bhogaḥ kartavyo bhavati taṃ taṃ kurvate | [KauśS, 14, 3 27.1]
ye parimokṣaṃ kāmayante te parimucyante | [KauśS, 14, 3 28.1]
{KauśS, 14, 4}
atha rājñām indramahasyopācārakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 1]
proṣṭhapade śuklapakṣe 'śvayuje vāṣṭamyāṃ praveśaḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 2]
śravaṇenotthāpanam | [KauśS, 14, 4 3]
saṃbhṛteṣu saṃbhāreṣu brahmā rājā cobhau snātāvahatavasanau surabhiṇau vratavantau karmaṇyāv upavasataḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 4]
śvo bhūte śaṃ no devyāḥ pādair ardharcābhyām ṛcā ṣaṭkṛtvodakam ācāmataḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 5]

athendram utthāpayanti | [KauśS, 14, 4 7]
ā tvāhārṣaṃ dhruvā dyaur viśas tvā sarvā vāñchantv iti sarvato 'pramattā dhārayeran | [KauśS, 14, 4 8]
adbhutaṃ hi vimānotthitam upatiṣṭhante | [KauśS, 14, 4 9]
abhibhūr yajña ity etais tribhiḥ sūktair anvārabdhe rājani pūrṇahomaṃ juhuyāt | [KauśS, 14, 4 10]
atha paśūnām upācāram | [KauśS, 14, 4 11]
indradevatāḥ syuḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 12]
ye rājño bhṛtyāḥ syuḥ sarve dīkṣitā brahmacāriṇaḥ syuḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 13]
indraṃ copasadya yajeraṃs trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā | [KauśS, 14, 4 14]
trir ayanam ahnām upatiṣṭhante haviṣā ca yajante | [KauśS, 14, 4 15]
āvṛta indram aham iti | [KauśS, 14, 4 16]
indra kṣatram iti haviṣo hutvā brāhmaṇān paricareyuḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 17]
na saṃsthitahomāñ juhuyād ity āhur ācāryāḥ | [KauśS, 14, 4 18]
indrasyāvabhṛthād indram avabhṛthāya vrajanti | [KauśS, 14, 4 19]
apāṃ sūktair āplutya pradakṣiṇam āvṛtyāpa upaspṛśyānavekṣamāṇāḥ pratyudāvrajanti | [KauśS, 14, 4 20]
brāhmaṇān bhaktenopepsanti | [KauśS, 14, 4 21]
śvaḥ śvo 'sya rāṣṭraṃ jyāyo bhavatyeko 'syāṃ pṛthivyāṃ rājā bhavati na purā jarasaḥ pramīyate ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān indramaheṇa carati | [KauśS, 14, 4 22]
{KauśS, 14, 5}
atha vedasyādhyayanavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | [KauśS, 14, 5 1.1]

evaṃ chandāṃsi | [KauśS, 14, 5 3.1]
lomnāṃ cānivartanam | [KauśS, 14, 5 4.1]

nirghāte | [KauśS, 14, 5 20.1]

ācāryaputrabhāryāś ca | [KauśS, 14, 5 29.1]
atha śiṣyaṃ sahādhyāyinam apradhānaguruṃ copasannam ahorātraṃ varjayet | [KauśS, 14, 5 30.1]

apartudaivam ākālam | [KauśS, 14, 5 32.1]

yac cānyad daivam adbhutaṃ sarvaṃ nirghātavad bhavet | [KauśS, 14, 5 33.2]
ṛtāv adhyāyaś chāndasaḥ kālpya āpartukaḥ smṛtaḥ | [KauśS, 14, 5 34.1]
